Validation Status: valid

## Summary
<h3>Breaking</h3>
<ul>
<li>Nodes/exec: remove the duplicated <code>nodes.run</code> shell wrapper from the CLI and agent <code>nodes</code> tool so node shell execution always goes through <code>exec host=node</code>, keeping node-specific capabilities on <code>nodes invoke</code> and the dedicated media/location/notify actions.</li>
<li>Plugin SDK: deprecate the legacy provider compat subpaths plus the older bundled provider setup and channel-runtime compatibility shims, emit migration warnings, and keep the current documented <code>openclaw/plugin-sdk/*</code> entrypoints plus local <code>api.ts</code> / <code>runtime-api.ts</code> barrels as the forward path ahead of a future major-release removal.</li>
<li>Skills/install and Plugins/install: built-in dangerous-code <code>critical</code> findings and install-time scan failures now fail closed by default, so plugin installs and gateway-backed skill dependency installs that previously succeeded may now require an explicit dangerous override such as <code>--dangerously-force-unsafe-install</code> to proceed.</li>
<li>Gateway/auth: <code>trusted-proxy</code> now rejects mixed shared-token configs, and local-direct fallback requires the configured token instead of implicitly authenticating same-host callers. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/zhangning-agent/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/zhangning-agent">@zhangning-agent</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jacobtomlinson/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jacobtomlinson">@jacobtomlinson</a>, and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Gateway/node commands: node commands now stay disabled until node pairing is approved, so device pairing alone is no longer enough to expose declared node commands. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4171565116" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/57777" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57777/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57777">#57777</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jacobtomlinson/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jacobtomlinson">@jacobtomlinson</a>.</li>
<li>Gateway/node events: node-originated runs now stay on a reduced trusted surface, so notification-driven or node-triggered flows that previously relied on broader host/session tool access may need adjustment. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4170388163" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/57691" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57691/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57691">#57691</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jacobtomlinson/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jacobtomlinson">@jacobtomlinson</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>ACP/plugins: add an explicit default-off ACPX plugin-tools MCP bridge config, document the trust boundary, and harden the built-in bridge packaging/logging path so global installs and stdio MCP sessions work reliably. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4163232065" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/56867" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/56867/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/56867">#56867</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/joe2643/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/joe2643">@joe2643</a>.</li>
<li>Agents/LLM: add a configurable idle-stream timeout for embedded runner requests so stalled model streams abort cleanly instead of hanging until the broader run timeout fires. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4142252345" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/55072" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/55072/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/55072">#55072</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/liuy/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/liuy">@liuy</a>.</li>
<li>Agents/MCP: materialize bundle MCP tools with provider-safe names (<code>serverName__toolName</code>), support optional <code>streamable-http</code> transport selection plus per-server connection timeouts, and preserve real tool results from aborted/error turns unless truncation explicitly drops them. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4092891606" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/49505" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49505/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49505">#49505</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ziomancer/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ziomancer">@ziomancer</a>.</li>
<li>Android/notifications: add notification-forwarding controls with package filtering, quiet hours, rate limiting, and safer picker behavior for forwarded notification events. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4041951103" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/40175" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/40175/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/40175">#40175</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nimbleenigma/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nimbleenigma">@nimbleenigma</a>.</li>
<li>Background tasks: turn tasks into a real shared background-run control plane instead of ACP-only bookkeeping by unifying ACP, subagent, cron, and background CLI execution under one SQLite-backed ledger, routing detached lifecycle updates through the executor seam, adding audit/maintenance/status visibility, tightening auto-cleanup and lost-run recovery, improving task awareness in internal status/tool surfaces, and clarifying the split between heartbeat/main-session automation and detached scheduled runs. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/mbelinky/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/mbelinky">@mbelinky</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Background tasks: add the first linear task flow control surface with <code>openclaw flows list|show|cancel</code>, keep manual multi-task flows separate from one-task auto-sync flows, and surface doctor recovery hints for obviously orphaned or broken flow/task linkage. ## Why It Matters
Source signal: <h3>Breaking</h3>
<ul>
<li>Nodes/exec: remove the duplicated <code>nodes.run</code> shell wrapper from the CLI and agent <code>nodes</code> tool so node shell execution always goes through <code>exec host=node</code>, keeping node-specific capabilities on <code>nodes invoke</code> and the dedicated media/location/notify actions.</li>
<li>Plugin SDK: deprecate the legacy provider compat subpaths plus the older bundled provider setup and channel-runtime compatibility shims, emit migration warnings, and keep the current documented <code>openclaw/plugin-sdk/*</code> entrypoints plus local <code>api.ts</code> / <code>runtime-api.ts</code> barrels as the forward path ahead of a future major-release removal.</li>
<li>Skills/install and Plugins/install: built-in dangerous-code <code>critical</code> findings and install-time scan failures now fail closed by default, so plugin installs and gateway-backed skill dependency installs that previously succeeded may now require an explicit dangerous override such as <code>--dangerously-force-unsafe-install</code> to proceed.</li>
<li>Gateway/auth: <code>trusted-proxy</code> now rejects mixed shared-token configs, and local-direct fallback requires the configured token instead of implicitly authenticating same-host callers. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/zhangning-agent/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/zhangning-agent">@zhangning-agent</a>, <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jacobtomlinson/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jacobtomlinson">@jacobtomlinson</a>, and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Gateway/node commands: node commands now stay disabled until node pairing is approved, so device pairing alone is no longer enough to expose declared node commands. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4171565116" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/57777" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57777/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57777">#57777</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jacobtomlinson/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jacobtomlinson">@jacobtomlinson</a>.</li>
<li>Gateway/node events: node-originated runs now stay on a reduced trusted surface, so notification-driven or node-triggered flows that previously relied on broader host/session tool access may need adjustment. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4170388163" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/57691" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57691/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57691">#57691</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jacobtomlinson/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jacobtomlinson">@jacobtomlinson</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3>Changes</h3>
<ul>
<li>ACP/plugins: add an explicit default-off ACPX plugin-tools MCP bridge config, document the trust boundary, and harden the built-in bridge packaging/logging path so global installs and stdio MCP sessions work reliably. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4163232065" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/56867" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/56867/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/56867">#56867</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/joe2643/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/joe2643">@joe2643</a>.</li>
<li>Agents/LLM: add a configurable idle-stream timeout for embedded runner requests so stalled model streams abort cleanly instead of hanging until the broader run timeout fires. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4142252345" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/55072" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/55072/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/55072">#55072</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/liuy/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/liuy">@liuy</a>.</li>
<li>Agents/MCP: materialize bundle MCP tools with provider-safe names (<code>serverName__toolName</code>), support optional <code>streamable-http</code> transport selection plus per-server connection timeouts, and preserve real tool results from aborted/error turns unless truncation explicitly drops them. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4092891606" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/49505" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49505/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/49505">#49505</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/ziomancer/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/ziomancer">@ziomancer</a>.</li>
<li>Android/notifications: add notification-forwarding controls with package filtering, quiet hours, rate limiting, and safer picker behavior for forwarded notification events. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4041951103" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/40175" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/40175/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/40175">#40175</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/nimbleenigma/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/nimbleenigma">@nimbleenigma</a>.</li>
<li>Background tasks: turn tasks into a real shared background-run control plane instead of ACP-only bookkeeping by unifying ACP, subagent, cron, and background CLI execution under one SQLite-backed ledger, routing detached lifecycle updates through the executor seam, adding audit/maintenance/status visibility, tightening auto-cleanup and lost-run recovery, improving task awareness in internal status/tool surfaces, and clarifying the split between heartbeat/main-session automation and detached scheduled runs. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/mbelinky/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/mbelinky">@mbelinky</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Background tasks: add the first linear task flow control surface with <code>openclaw flows list|show|cancel</code>, keep manual multi-task flows separate from one-task auto-sync flows, and surface doctor recovery hints for obviously orphaned or broken flow/task linkage. Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/mbelinky/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/mbelinky">@mbelinky</a> and <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/vincentkoc/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/vincentkoc">@vincentkoc</a>.</li>
<li>Channels/QQ Bot: add QQ Bot as a bundled channel plugin with multi-account setup, SecretRef-aware credentials, slash commands, reminders, and media send/receive support. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4121906239" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/52986" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/52986/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/52986">#52986</a>) Thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/sliverp/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/sliverp">@sliverp</a>.</li>
<li>Diffs: skip unused viewer-versus-file SSR preload work so <code>diffs</code> view-only and file-only runs do less render work while keeping mode outputs aligned. (<a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="4173608505" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/issues/57909" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57909/hovercard" href="https://github.com/openclaw/openclaw/pull/57909">#57909</a>) thanks <a class="user-mention notranslate" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/gumadeiras/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/gumadeiras">@gumadeiras</a>.</li>
